```sql

    ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY (SELECT NULL)) AS RowNumber,
    EXPAND_STANDARD_BOM_DANJIE_KAYLA.*

    dbo.EXPAND_STANDARD_BOM_DANJIE_KAYLA
```
